posted:Posted February 17, 2024
msg:I took my family out for the Spring Festival and booked a deluxe king-size bed room. The actual pictures and the room I stayed in seemed more like a superior king-size bed room. When I checked in, I emphasized that I wanted a quieter room. The front desk arranged it on the 3rd floor with a sincere attitude and told me that it would definitely be quiet. The room number was 8348 and the other was 8343 (where my parents lived). The next day, my parents told us that it was very noisy at night, like the sound of an engine or boiler. It was very loud in the middle of the night and they didn't sleep well. We went to their room to find out and found that there was noise in the corridor on the 3rd floor, and the smaller the room number, the louder it was. Considering that we were going out to play in the morning, I moved my parents' luggage to my room at 8 o'clock, and then went to the front desk to report the problem of my parents' room. Because the elderly are in poor health, I hope the hotel will coordinate and solve it. The front desk manager is a man. He checked their hotel check-in system and told me that the guests next door at 8347 or 8349 would check out that day, and they would arrange one of the rooms for us to change. We were very grateful. After breakfast, I went back to my room and saw the guests at 8347 checking out with their suitcases when I went out. I thought it was probably this room. Then I returned the room card of room 8343 to the front desk, and went to play with peace of mind.
At around 2 pm, we went back to the hotel to ask the front desk if we could get a new room key, but we were told that all the two reserved rooms were extended, and only room 8346 could be arranged (when I was told that all the rooms were extended, my mind was full of question marks, because I saw a room checked out with my own eyes in the morning). We asked to go to the new room first, but there was still a sound in the afternoon. Then I called the front desk again and asked if room 8347 and room 8349 were indeed occupied. I was told that they were occupied, but one of them was checked out and newly checked in, and the other was extended. This reply was different from the waiter who asked us at the front desk when we came back. I was very unhappy at once. First of all, you promised to reserve it for me, but you didnâ€™t reserve it and didnâ€™t call me in advance. You still fooled me after you came back. Secondly, I said that the old man didnâ€™t sleep all night and was in poor health and hoped to solve it, but you just perfunctorily told me. I asked for a room on another floor with a similar location to mine to be arranged. They said they could look at the room. I asked the lobby manager to solve it. Soon, a manager named Xia took the room card of 6847 and showed us the room. This room was very quiet, so we chose this one. After telling Manager Xia the whole story, she also told us that the 6th floor was indeed quieter than the 3rd floor. She also said that she would give a gift to apologize when we checked out (the gift was not important, and she did not tell us what the gift was. We did not ask what it was. As long as the problem of the elderly was solved, it would be fine).
We checked out on the morning of the 17th. When we left, the front desk staff who checked out at the front desk did not tell us that there was a gift at the first time. It was another waiter standing next to us who stopped us and said that we would give us a gift. It turned out to be a box of steamed buns from the Garden Tea House! We expressed our gratitude, but because we did not see Manager Xia himself, we could only express it in the evaluation!
The hotel was quite satisfactory, and the cleaning auntie was also very nice, but the reception ability and service quality of the front desk really need to be improved. I think integrity is the most important thing. Many things promised to customers should not be changed easily. Even if there is an emergency, you should contact the customer as soon as possible to inform the reason. Everyone will understand and sympathize, instead of just making do with it! 
We are deeply pleased with the patience and sincerity of the lobby manager. Thank you again!

Maybe the hotel is a bit older. Luxury 5 stars may not be the kind of 5 stars in my heart. It still belongs to the category of old 5 stars. The total floor is 6th floor. On the 5th floor, there is an east that resembles a sky garden, where you can enjoy the sun in winter Very good, it is too hot in summer, and the sanitary condition is good. I have been seeing the staff wiping it all the time.
The breakfast in the hotel does not have too many varieties, but it is delicious, but ms does not fit the feeling of a 5-star hotel. Maybe because of the garden restaurant next to it, not many people dine in the hotel.
I ate dinner on the second floor of the hotel on the day I was too lazy. The price is affordable, the dishes are large, and there are discounts for in-house guests. I madly call the soft-pocket bottom vegetable-leek, how can it be so tender!
If you drive by yourself, the hotel provides free parking coupons, which is highly praised.
